[CREATURE:TB_DND_CAMBION_EVILREGION]
	[DESCRIPTION:Born of mixed fiendish and mortal parentage, Cambions are, unlike regular half-fiends, inherently evil and possess quite a few magical powers. They are easy to identify, having tails, horns, leathery wings and exotic skin colours. Cambions instinctively seek to dominate and corrupt those around them.]
